<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、內取蘊，對於五蘊，認為有我，會生起「我慢」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、已得未得顛倒，錯認自己所證得的境界，沒有得到禪定，認為得到禪定；沒有得到初果，認為得到初果，對已經得到的或沒有得到的功德，有錯亂、顛倒，稱為「增上慢」。這都是因為沒有認知清楚。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、功德顛倒，沒有功德的地方認為有功德，稱為「邪慢」。例如造鬼神的廟自認有功德，事實上沒有很大功德，卻認為做這件事有功德。這些在〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷55，1819頁曾說過。這裡所說的前三，是指三慢類，相對於自己，於劣有情有慢、於等有情有過慢、於勝有情有慢過慢及卑慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、於受欲處慢</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於受欲處慢，說明於受欲處生慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於受用欲處慢者，謂由大財、大族、大徒眾等現在前故，心遂高舉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於受用欲處有高慢的人，是指由於財富很多、家族旺盛、有很多弟子與徒眾現前的時候，與他人相比，有如意自在的感覺，心就高舉而生慢心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、於後有處慢</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科於後有處慢，說明於後有處生慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於後有處慢者，謂由計我當有不有，廣說乃至我當非想非非想等，若動不動，戲論造作諸愛趣中，現前轉故，心遂高舉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於後有處慢方面，是指依常見執著我死後將來會有某類可愛的生命體繼續存在，或依斷見執著我死後就永遠斷滅，乃至我死後將來生到非想非非想處等而生於慢；若是依於常見起慢計有快樂的世間，名為動，於斷見起慢執著未來不續，名為無動。依我我所等戲論分別生在三界五趣可愛果報處中，令心高舉而生起高慢。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、不惑亂慢及惑亂慢3　申一、約七慢辨2　酉一、不惑亂慢</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科不惑亂慢及惑亂慢，說明不惑亂慢及惑亂慢，分三科；第一科約七慢辨，約七慢分辨不惑亂慢及惑亂慢，又分二科；第一科不惑亂慢，說明不惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不惑亂慢者，謂於下劣計己為勝、於等計等而生憍慢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不惑亂的高慢有二種情形。第一種是於下劣計己為勝，對於在財富上、族姓、智慧或者是徒眾等，事實上比自己下劣的眾生，自己認為比這類下劣的眾生殊勝，因而生起高慢，這是不惑亂慢。第二種是於等計等，不管在財富、族姓、智慧或者是徒眾等，事實上自己與對方差不多，而自己也認為與對方差不多，心中生起的憍慢，也是屬於不惑亂慢。這二種情況都符合事實，合起來稱為不惑亂慢。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂於下劣計己為勝等者：慢有七種，謂慢、過慢、慢過慢、我慢、增上慢、下劣慢、邪慢。今說初一慢名不惑亂慢。集論中說：慢者，謂於下劣計己為勝，或於相似計己相似，心舉為性。（集論四卷十頁）所餘六慢名惑亂慢，亦如集論一一別釋應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　高慢有七種，指慢、過慢、慢過慢、我慢、增上慢、下劣慢、邪慢。前面已經解釋這些慢，將七種慢歸納為二類，這裡解釋第一類與事實符合的稱為不惑亂慢，其它六種慢，不符合實際的情況都稱為惑亂慢。《集論》卷4，10頁中說：慢，是指於下劣計執自己為殊勝，或於相似計執自己與他相似，心高舉為性。所餘六種慢名惑亂慢，也如《集論》一一各別解釋，應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、惑亂慢</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科惑亂慢，說明惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4710"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">惑亂慢者，謂餘六慢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　惑亂慢方面，是指其餘六種慢。過慢，是指於各種條件實際上與自已相等的有情，但自己卻認為超過對方，沒有看清事實真相，這當中有迷惑，因迷惑生起的高慢心，稱為惑亂慢。對於殊勝的有情，生起慢過慢，過慢，乃至卑慢（下劣慢）。慢過慢是對於超過自己的有情，卻認為自己超過對方，這是不符合事實；過慢是對於超過自己的有情，卻認為自己與對方相等，這也是不符合事實；及對超過自己很多的有情，卻認為自己只有差一點而已，這樣的卑慢不符合事實，這些都稱為惑亂慢。其次是我慢，五蘊中沒有常住、不變、有主宰的我，認為有我，這是不符合事實的，也是惑亂慢。未得謂得，未證謂證的增上慢，不符合事實，也是惑亂慢。邪慢，是顛倒功德，不符合事實，也稱為惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、約受用資具辨2　酉一、惑亂慢</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約受用資具辨，約受用資具辨明不惑亂慢及惑亂慢，分二科；第一科惑亂慢，說明受用資具的惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由受用鄙劣資具，自謂富樂，名惑亂慢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由受用粗俗下劣的資具，自己卻認為很高貴、很富樂，這是不符合事實而生起的高慢心，稱為惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、不惑亂慢</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不惑亂慢，說明受用資具的不惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若由受用勝妙資具，自謂富樂，名不惑亂慢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一種人事實上受用殊勝微妙的資具，自己認為有錢，也很快樂，這種人名為不惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、約計後有辨2　酉一、惑亂慢</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約計後有辨，約執著後有辨明不惑亂慢及惑亂慢，分二科；第一科惑亂慢，說明執著後有之惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由邪行，謂後有勝，名惑亂慢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於造作錯誤顛倒的行為，卻認為下一生的果報會很殊勝，這種不符合事實而生起的高慢心，稱為惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、不惑亂慢</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不惑亂慢，說明執著後有之不惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若由正行，謂後有勝，名不惑亂慢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果一生都修五戒、十善，規規矩矩，自己認為下一生的果報會很殊勝，這種高慢心符合事實，是不惑亂慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳八、無明2　午一、標相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科無明，說明無明的行相，分二科；第一科標相，標出無明的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="48689:46645"></a>無明者，謂於所知真實覺悟能覆、能障，心所為性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無明方面，是指對於所知的蘊界處真實的情況，沒有辦法覺悟，一種覆障有情的心所，使有情沒辦法了知一切法無我、無我所的事實與真理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、辨類2　未一、四種2　申一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨類，辨別無明的種類，分二科；第一科四種，說明四種無明，又分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出四種無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4711"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此略四種。一、無解愚，二、放逸愚，三、染汙愚，四、不染汙愚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無明要略而言有四種。一、無解愚，因不了解所知事實相而生的無明；二、放逸愚，因不精進斷惡生善引生的無明；三、染汙愚，因煩惱障未斷引生的無明；四、不染汙愚，因所知障未斷引生的無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、隨釋4　酉一、無解愚</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋四種無明，分四科；第一科無解愚，解釋無解愚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於不見聞覺知所知義中所有無智，名無解愚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是對於不曾見聞覺知的無我義，沒有智慧理解，名為無解愚。例如不曾觀察五蘊無我，就不能證入諸法實相，對五蘊就會有無解愚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、放逸愚</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科放逸愚，解釋放逸愚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於見聞覺知所知義中散亂失念所有無智，名放逸愚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於已經有見聞覺知所了解蘊、處、界等諸法諸義中，由於散亂、失念，常常忘失正念、失去智慧，稱為放逸愚。這是因為不精進引起的愚癡無明。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、染汙愚</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科染汙愚，解釋染汙愚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於顛倒心所有無智，名染汙愚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　顛倒心，是指於世間法無常謂常、於苦謂樂、於無我謂有我、於不淨謂淨，這一類由常樂我淨的執著心，所生的愚痴與顛倒想相應，稱為染汙愚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、不染汙愚</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科不染汙愚，解釋不染汙愚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不顛倒心所有無智，名不染汙愚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不顛倒心，是指這類有情沒有常樂我淨的顛倒，但是有法執無明，不了達法無我故，有法執相應的顛倒與無智，稱為不染汙愚。阿羅漢還有不染汙無知，染汙愚是指凡夫，不染汙愚是指二乘的阿羅漢及辟支佛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於顛倒心所有無智等者：非我計我，是名顛倒。彼心相應所有無智，名染汙愚，此即我執無明。離我顛倒，法執相應所有無智，名不染汙愚，此即法執無明。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五蘊不是常住、不變、有主宰的我，執著是我，稱為顛倒。這一念心與我執相應引生的無智，稱為染汙愚，這就是我執無明。遠離我執顛倒，由法執相應引生的無智，稱為不染汙愚，這就是法執無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、二種2　申一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科二種，說明無明有二種，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出二種無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此無明總有二種。一、煩惱相應無明，二、獨行無明。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這類無明心所有二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、無明心所有時與貪瞋等煩惱相應，稱為煩惱相應無明；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、無明心所有時候不與貪瞋等相應，稱為獨行無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、隨釋2　酉一、煩惱相應無明</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋二種無明，分二科；第一科煩惱相應，解釋煩惱相應無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4712"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">非無愚癡而起諸惑，是故貪等餘惑相應所有無明，名煩惱相應無明。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　並不是沒有愚癡而能生起種種的煩惱，因此與貪等其他煩惱相應的無明，名為煩惱相應無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、獨行無明</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科獨行無明，解釋獨行無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若無貪等諸煩惱纏，但於苦等諸諦境中，由不如理作意力故，鈍慧士夫補特伽羅，諸不如實簡擇、覆障、纏裹、闇昧等心所性，名獨行無明。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是沒有與貪瞋等根本煩惱相應的無明，只是在苦集滅道四諦等所緣境中，由不如理作意的力量，屬於鈍根下劣智慧的士夫補特伽羅（士夫就是補特伽羅、就是人），不能如實簡擇四諦的道理，有迷於事理的煩惱所覆障，纏繞著，使心闇昧，這樣的心所性質稱為獨行無明。無明分有二種，一種是共無明，一種是不共無明。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、共無明，指前六識與貪等根本煩惱相應的無明，稱為共無明。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、不共無明又分成二種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 獨行不共無明，與第六識相應但不與貪等根本煩惱相應的無明，又分為二種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（1）主獨行不共無明，是第六識與大隨八種煩惱、中隨二種煩惱俱起，而未顯這類煩惱體用，單獨顯此無明之體用。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（2）非主獨行不共無明，第六識與忿等小隨煩惱俱起，小隨煩惱之體用顯，無明之體用隱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 恆行不共無明，與第七末那識相應之無明。此無明乃一切凡夫無始以來相續不斷者，與我見、我愛、我慢三根本煩惱相應，能障礙真義智，稱為恆行不共無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳九、疑2　午一、標體性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科疑，說明疑的行相，分二科；第一科標體性，標出疑的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">疑者，猶豫二分不決定，心所為性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　疑，是指內心猶豫不決分成二分。「二」，是指對於諸法實相的有與無二個部分，心無法決定：諸法實相是真實有？還是假有？或對於事情是這樣？還是那樣？是此？或彼？二分，心不決定，這種心所，稱為疑。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明建立，說明疑由五相差別建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此疑，略由五相差別建立。謂於他世作用、因、果、諸諦、寶中，心懷猶豫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道疑，要略而言可以由他世、作用、因果、諸諦、三寶中、心懷猶豫五種相貌來建立它的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、他世：對過去或未來的境界生起疑惑，倒底有沒有過去生或未來世？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、作用：懷疑有沒有化生有情（中有）及懷疑父母與胞胎的作用等？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、因果：懷疑有沒有在因地的妙行惡行的差別？有沒有善行、功德等可愛樂果法？懷疑有沒有由惡行招感苦的等流果及異熟果？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、諸諦，懷疑苦集滅道四諦是真實不虛的嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、寶中，懷疑在佛法僧三寶中有沒有什麼功德？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對三世及因緣所生的五蘊等事及四諦三寶等，於事於理心中懷疑、猶豫不決，稱為疑。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在《法華經玄贊要集》卷2有引本論之文解釋疑的五相：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、疑他世，懷疑過去世及未來世有佛法僧三寶否？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、疑作用，懷疑父母及胞胎之作用、化生有情之作用、中有身傳識之作用。人死後有無中有？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、疑因，不知善因感善果，惡因感惡果，懷疑布施是富貴因，慳貪是貧窮因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、疑果，懷疑有無異熟果及沙門果等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、疑諦寶，懷疑苦集滅道四諦及佛法僧三寶為有為無？這是通疑理事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　關於第五點，根據《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷6〈1 諦品〉說：「疑結，是指於四諦心有猶豫，疑的煩惱所繫縛故，於佛法僧寶三寶妄生疑惑；因為疑惑故，於三寶所不修正行；因為於三寶所不修正行故，廣行不善、不行諸善，由此能招未來世苦與苦相應。」懷疑四諦也就會懷疑三寶。《成唯識論》卷6說：疑，是指於諸諦理猶豫為性，能障不疑善品為業。因為猶豫的人不能生善法。《百法論顯幽鈔》卷7解釋這一段文：「於諸諦理猶豫為性，所謂諦理，是指四諦道理的真理，或世俗、勝義二諦道理的真理。於四諦理及事等都生猶豫不定，懷疑是實有？還是實無？依此《百法論顯幽鈔》卷7說：疑於五相而起。一者他世、二作用、三者因果、四者四諦、五者三寶。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論》雖只說諦理，也能含攝本論五相。若是懷疑於過去、未來他世有無苦果（五蘊），屬於四諦中苦諦所攝。懷疑作用，是懷疑有沒有中有等，及中有是否有傳識之作用？屬於四諦因果所攝。懷疑因果，懷疑有沒有因果，屬於四諦因果所攝。懷疑四諦因果有二種，若是有漏因果，即苦諦集諦二諦所攝；若是無漏因果，即滅諦道諦二諦所攝。若說懷疑四諦，是對世間及出世間因果生起疑惑。若說懷疑三寶，是滅諦道諦二諦所攝。《成唯識論》雖只說諦理，也能含攝本論五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》略由五相差別建立等者：於他世中流轉作用，心懷猶豫，是名初相。如是於彼妙行、惡行差別因性及彼果性，於四聖諦及佛法僧，心懷猶豫，如其次第名後四相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於他世中流轉作用，是指對於有沒有過去世或未來世這件事情，心懷猶豫，這稱為初相。因此對於有沒有妙行惡行的差別因性及果性，於四聖諦及佛法僧三寶，心懷猶豫，如所說次第，稱為後四相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、廣辨4　辰一、辨能緣3　巳一、標緣二種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科廣辨，詳細辨別十種煩惱差別，分四科；第一科辨能緣，辨別十種煩惱能緣的對象，又分三科；第一科標緣二種，標出十種煩惱能緣事及煩惱二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="47844:46672"></a>如是所說十種煩惱，亦緣事轉、亦緣煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上面所說的薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見、見取見、戒禁取見、貪、恚、慢、無明和疑，這十種煩惱有的是緣五蘊、十二處、十八界這些因緣所生事而現前，有時候是緣著內心分別的煩惱而現前，因此說亦緣事轉、亦緣煩惱轉。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4713"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋其差別2　午一、約自地辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋其差別，解釋十種煩惱緣事及煩惱差別，分二科；第一科約自地辨，約自地煩惱說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂十煩惱皆與自地一切煩惱展轉相緣，亦緣自地諸有漏事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這十種煩惱都與自地一切煩惱展轉相緣，也緣自地種種有漏事而轉。欲界眾生十種煩惱都與欲界自地一切煩惱展轉相緣，也緣著欲界的眼耳鼻舌身、男女等欲界有漏的煩惱事而轉；色界、無色界天的人，他們沒有瞋煩惱，其餘九種煩惱與自地一切煩惱展轉相緣，也緣自地色界有漏的五蘊或無色界四蘊而轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、約上下地辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約上下地辨，約上下地辨別煩惱緣事及煩惱的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">下地煩惱能緣上地煩惱及事，非上地惑能緣下地煩惱及事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　上地是指色界、無色界，下地是欲界。欲界的眾生能夠緣到上地，能夠緣色無色界的煩惱及有漏事，下地眾生的煩惱很廣。上地的眾生只緣色無色界的煩惱，並不緣下地的煩惱及有漏事。《瑜伽論記》說這是約隨順理門，基本上是隨順小乘教而言。在〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷59決擇，有說到上地的眾生，也可以緣下地的煩惱及事而起慢心。卷59中又說：「他境緣，謂色界於欲行煩惱，無色界於色行煩惱。又復下地於上地煩惱，所以者何？生上地者於彼下地諸有情所，由常恒樂淨具勝功德自謂為勝故。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、結不廣說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結不廣說，結說煩惱展轉相緣及下地煩惱能緣上地煩惱，餘決擇文不再細說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是煩惱展轉相緣，及下地惑能緣上地。於此處所餘決擇文，更不復現。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是在前面的地方沒有提到的，緣起法的特性是此有故彼有，一法引生一法，展轉相緣，決無不靠眾緣、單獨存在之一法可得。煩惱也是一樣，生起一種煩惱也會展轉引生其他煩惱，煩惱與煩惱之間彼此相依、相互引發，展轉相緣、相生；及下地的煩惱也能往上延伸到上地去，也能緣上地煩惱。有下地煩惱的人也一定具有上二地的煩惱種子。生到上二界，有上地煩惱的人，原有下地的煩惱已調伏不現行，只有緣自地煩惱及事。有關煩惱的能緣就說到這裡，其他決擇文不會再出現。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》下地煩惱能緣上地煩惱及事者：此上地緣，當知唯自分別所起名境，非彼下地煩惱親緣上地，不同分界故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界下地眾生的煩惱緣著色無色界，只能緣著分別心所現起來的能詮的名及名所詮的境，並不是欲界眾生下地的煩惱緣著上地的煩惱時，能親緣那件事情。能緣著上地的事及煩惱是分別所起，內心生起這樣的想法，依名言現出那樣的境界。因為界地不同，不是親緣，只能緣分別心所起的名言境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、辨性別2　巳一、總辨二性2　午一、舉薩迦耶見2　未一、俱生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨性別，辨別煩惱善性，惡性，無記性三性及俱生、分別二性的差別，分二科；第一科總辨二性，總辨俱生及分別二性，又分二科；第一科舉薩迦耶見，舉薩迦耶見二性為例，又分二科；第一科俱生，說明俱生薩迦耶見的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，俱生薩迦耶見唯無記性，數現行故，非極損惱自他處故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，俱生起的薩迦耶見（我見）是屬於無記性，常常、任運現行，由於屬於無記性，因此不會很強力的損惱自己及他人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論》卷1：「我執略有二種。一者俱生、二者分別。俱生我執，無始時來虛妄熏習內因力故恒與身俱，不待邪教及邪分別任運而轉，故名俱生。此復二種，一常相續在第七識，緣第八識起自心相執為實我。二有間斷，在第六識，緣識所變五取蘊相，或總或別起自心相執為實我。此二我執細故難斷，後修道中數數修習勝生空觀方能除滅。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、分別2　申一、在欲界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科分別，說明分別起的薩迦耶見，分二科；第一科在欲界，說明分別起的薩迦耶見在欲界的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4714"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若分別起薩迦耶見，由堅執故，與前相違。在欲界者，唯不善性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若分別生起的我見，由於非常堅固執著，與俱生的、無記性的薩迦耶見不一樣。欲界的眾生，分別起的我見是屬於不善的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論》卷1：「分別我執亦由現在外緣力故非與身俱，要待邪教及邪分別然後方起故名分別，唯在第六意識中有。此亦二種，一緣邪教所說蘊相起自心相分別計度執為實我。二緣邪教所說我相，起自心相分別計度執為實我。此二我執麁故易斷，初見道時觀一切法生空真如即能除滅。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、在上地</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科在上地，上二地分別起的薩迦耶見的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若在上地，奢摩他力所制持故，多白淨法所攝受故，成無記性。由染汙故，體是隱沒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若在色、無色界分別起的薩迦耶見，由於有奢摩他的定力能夠控制分別起的薩迦耶見，使其不常現起，又因為色無色界有情沒有瞋心，多數是白淨善法所攝受故，成為無記性；但此薩迦耶見以染汙慧為體性，障礙成就聖道，屬於有覆，因此色、無色界分別起的薩迦耶見是有覆無記性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例所餘煩惱</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例所餘煩惱，例說所餘煩惱二性也同薩迦耶見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所餘煩惱，由此道理，隨應當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其他的煩惱，由這種道理，隨所相應的應該也能了解。這是說明薩迦耶見的道理，以薩迦耶見為例，其他的九種煩惱類推可知，就不多說了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由染汙故體是隱沒者：謂彼俱生、若分別起薩迦耶見，由染汙慧為其體性，故彼無記是有覆攝，名是隱沒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　俱生薩迦耶見及分別起的薩迦耶見，都由染汙慧為它的體性，雖然是無記性，還會障礙成就聖道，是有覆所攝，所以名為隱沒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、廣不善性2　午一、由起惡行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣不善性，詳細辨明不善性煩惱，分二科；第一科由起惡行，由能生起惡行故成不善性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲界煩惱為諸惡行安足處故，多不善性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界眾生如果生起煩惱，通常會生起惡行，煩惱是惡行依止安住的地方，因此多是不善性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、由往惡趣4　未一、標簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由往惡趣，由能往惡趣故成不善性，分四科；第一科標簡，標出能往惡趣的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又不善者，具三因緣能往惡趣，餘則不定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又不善性的煩惱，必須具足三種因緣才能夠到惡趣去受生，其它就不一定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4715"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》具三因緣能往惡趣等者：此說能往惡趣。惡不善法由具三種因緣，則定能往。所餘煩惱非不善性，不具三種能往惡趣因緣，則不決定往生惡趣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處說欲界煩惱能往惡趣，成為不善性。欲界煩惱能產生惡行，這些不善法如果具足三種因緣，決定會到惡道去。其他的煩惱沒有具足這三種因緣，不會到惡趣去。或者說，其他的煩惱不是不善性，不具足三種能往惡趣的因緣，不決定往生惡趣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、徵問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵問，提出問題發問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為三？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪三種因緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、別釋3　申一、第一因緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科別釋，各別解釋三種因緣，分三科；第一科第一因緣，往生惡趣的第一種因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂極多修習，殷重、無間計為功德，不見其失、不見其患，縱情而起，是初因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　當欲界眾生有惡不善法時，又常常生起這種煩惱，很周全完備而且沒有間斷的重覆生起，還認這種煩惱的想法是有功德的，沒有看到煩惱的過失，不知煩惱有什麼過患，甚至還放縱自己的心毫不遮攔，隨境即生起煩惱，這是第一種因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、第二因緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二因緣，往生惡趣的第二種因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">用此煩惱以為依處，由身語意，於諸惡行作及增長，是第二因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　用這種極為有力、時常串習的不善性煩惱為依止處，由身語意三業造作種種惡行，造作惡行之外還繼續增長惡行，這是第二種因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、第三因緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第三因緣，往往生惡趣的第三種因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此煩惱斷他善品，授不善品，是第三因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由這樣的煩惱斷除他人的善根，進一步教導他人這樣做，宣說這些惡法是對的。這是第三種因緣。例如恐怖份子宣說殺人可以生天，恐怖份子有這樣的信仰，也教他人這樣做惡行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》斷他善品授不善品者：謂如諸邪見者，宣說、開示、建立彼所說義，令他隨轉，由是因緣，斷他善根、生他邪見故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類邪見的人或者是邪見的宗教，宣說、開示、建立所主張的邪知邪見的義理，令他人隨他們所說的一起造作惡行，由此因緣，斷掉他人的善根，令他人產生邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、簡非</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科簡非，此處簡除順後受業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4716"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">除先所作能往惡趣順後受業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　另外一種到惡趣受果，是因為過去生造了到惡趣受果的順後受業，今生先受到人的果報後，下一生才到惡道去。此處簡除不是上一生的順後受業的因緣往惡趣受果。順後受業，是指現在世所造作之善惡業將於下下一生（第三生）才受或者是下下幾生才受果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》除先所作能往惡趣順後受業者：前說三種因緣，唯約現法不善煩惱為論。然先所作能往惡趣順後受業，非能定往惡趣，此不具論，是故除之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說三種因緣，只是約現在色受想行識中生起不善的煩惱，又具足三種因緣而論。還有一種是由過去生所做的能往惡趣的，但是不是下一生就受，是下下一生才受果的順後受業，這裡沒有特別提出來討論，所以簡除順後受業的情形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、辨相應2　巳一、六識相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨相應，辨明六識及五受與十種煩惱相應的差別，分二科；第一科六識相應，說明十煩惱中與六識相應的部分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又十煩惱，七唯意地，貪、恚、無明亦通五識。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又十種煩惱中除了貪恚無明以外的七種煩惱：薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見、見取見、戒禁取見、慢和疑，只有在〈意地〉的第六識會生起，貪恚無明也通於前五識。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、五受相應2　午一、舉於欲界2　未一、辨一一</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科五受相應，說明五受與十種煩惱相應的情形，分二科；第一科舉於欲界，舉出於欲界與五受相應的情形，又分二科；第一科辨一一，一一辨別欲界煩惱與受相應情形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於欲界，四見及慢，喜、捨相應；</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又於欲界的薩迦耶見、邊執見、見取見、戒禁取見，四種見及慢，與喜受、捨受相應。這是從多分來說，深細觀察就不一定是這樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》四見及慢喜捨相應者：於五見中除其邪見，所餘四見及慢，喜、捨相應，由彼邪見下別說故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於薩迦耶見、邊執見、見取見、戒禁取見、邪見五見中，除掉邪見以外，所餘四種見及高慢心都會與喜受、捨受相應，邪見下面會各別說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">貪，樂、喜、捨相應；恚，苦、憂、捨相應；邪見，喜、憂、捨相應；疑，憂、捨相應；無明，一切五根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　貪心時與樂受、喜受、捨受相應；瞋恚時有苦受、憂受、捨受相應；邪見時，有喜受、有憂受、捨受相應；懷疑是憂捨相應；無明與苦受、樂受、憂受、喜受、捨受等五受根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、明所說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明所說，說明煩惱與諸受相應的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此據多分相應道理，其餘深細，後當廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡只是根據大部分的情況來說，其他比較深細的道理，以後還會再解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4717"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例上諸地</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例上諸地，推例上地受根與煩惱相應情形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於上諸地隨所有根，即與彼地煩惱相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色無色界天的人隨所具足的受根，與自地的煩惱相應。色界初靜慮地及第二靜慮地有喜樂捨三受，第三靜慮地有樂捨二受，第四靜慮地及四空天有唯捨受相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》其餘深細後當廣說者：如下分別：是諸煩惱，幾與樂根相應？乃至幾與捨根相應？名約巨細道理建立，令久行者了自他身種種行解差別轉故。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/59.htm#46724:47599">陵本五十九卷四頁4793</a>）其義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如下文分別：這些煩惱，哪些與樂根相應？乃至哪些與捨根相應？說明煩惱與五受根相應的情況，稱為深細道理建立，令久修行的人能夠明白自己與他人種種心行差別的情況。在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷59，1950頁有說，道理可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、辨所緣2　巳一、有事無事別2　午一、無事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科辨所緣，辨別十種煩惱所緣差別，分二科；第一科有事無事別，所緣有事與無事的差別，又分二科；第一科無事，說明緣無事的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="47829:46726"></a>又十煩惱，見所斷者，名曰無事，彼所緣事非成實故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又十種煩惱中，見道所要斷的煩惱稱為無事，因為它多分是分別起的理惑、對因緣所生法為空的道理產生迷惑而生，所緣境非世俗實有的事。譬如薩迦耶見、邊執見、戒禁取等這些所分別的道理，沒有世俗實有的事，所以說是無事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、有事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有事，說明緣有事的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所餘煩惱有事，無事彼相違故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所餘修所斷煩惱緣有事及無事而起，無事與彼有事是相反的，因為無事惑是迷理所生，有事惑是迷事所生。這是麤相建立，大略而說。若綜合卷8、及58、59決擇所說，可以看出來，本論主要依分別起或俱生起的十種煩惱來說見所斷及修所斷的煩惱差別。這裡的「所餘煩惱有事無事」一段文，《披尋記》的作者有不同的看法，認為「無事」應該不要存在，懷疑可能是衍文。應該是「所餘煩惱有事」，「無事」是多出來的，認為修所斷的煩惱如貪恚慢無明，是緣有事生起的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》解釋：依諸煩惱所緣境的有無，來判斷有事無事。古代大德有三種不同的解釋如下：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種說法是：只有身見、邊執見、我慢這三種是無事惑，沒有真實的事情，只是內心分別生起的煩惱，其他的都稱為有事惑。如果依這樣來判斷，見所斷與修所斷的煩惱都通於有事、無事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種說法是：薩迦耶見、邊執見、見取見、戒禁取見這些執著是執有，是增益的，是屬於無事；邪見是謗無、執無，是損減的，是屬於無事。另外貪恚慢無明和疑就是有事了。這種解釋，見所斷和修所斷二種煩惱，也一樣通於有事無事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種說法是：約迷事理以辨有無。見所斷的是名無事，因為是分別心所生起的，迷理生惑，不是迷事。見所斷的煩惱乃是不了解因緣所生法的蘊界處無我的道理，這是對道理不瞭解而生起煩惱，所以說見所斷的煩惱稱為無事。修所斷的煩惱稱為有事，因為它是迷事生惑、或是俱生起的種種煩惱，包括薩迦耶見、邊執見乃至貪恚慢無明。披尋記的作者比較同意第三種說法，見道所斷的煩惱是無事，修道所斷的煩惱是有事。這是根据迷理，或者是迷事來說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有事是指所緣境是世俗實有的事，屬於事惑；無事是指能緣心所產生非正確的分別，屬於理惑。又十種煩惱中，見道所要斷的煩惱稱為無事，因為它多分是分別起的理惑、對因緣所生法為空的道理產生迷惑而生，所緣境非世俗實有的事。譬如薩迦耶見、邊執見、戒禁取等這些所分別的道理，沒有世俗實有的事，所以說是無事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是有事？什麼是無事？有事是指所緣境乃世俗實有的事，如肚子餓時生出想吃食物的貪心，這是有事。如果是思想上的問題名無事。沒有這件事卻去分別，這時煩惱生起的所緣境，稱為無事。凡夫緣的都是遍計所執，遍計所執有二種，一種是遍計外緣所生法的事，一種是由思惟分別而生起的。此外，現量上有迷惑名有事，比量上有迷惑名無事。若看到這朵花很喜歡，這是有事的煩惱。若看到這朵花覺得比那朵花更好，好不好因人而異不一定，是無事。見道所要斷的煩惱，這裡說是無事。修道所要斷的煩惱包括有事無事二種，披尋記的作者認為只有一種，應該只有有事。這段文比較深細，前面說過有三種，有人認為見道與修道所要斷的煩惱都包括有事無事。事實上煩惱的生起是很深細的，各種情況都會生起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此外有事又可以名為事，無事又可以名為理。有事煩惱指事惑，無事煩惱指理惑。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　據《佛光大辭典》說：事，指事相、事法；理，指真理、理性。於佛教中，事、理之相對意義有二；一、凡夫依迷情所見之事相，稱為事；聖者依智見所通達之真理，稱為理。而此所謂之「真理」，則依各宗派之說而有不同，或指四諦之理，或指真空之理，或指中道之理。二、視之為現象與本體之相對，即以森羅差別之現象事法，稱為事；以此等現象之本體乃平等無差別之理性真如，稱為理。而此現象之事與本體之理，二者之關係，各家立說不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、分取全取別2　午一、取一分事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科分取全取別，辨別煩惱所緣分取與全取的差別，分二科；第一科取一分事，說明煩惱取一分事為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="47824:46730"></a>又貪與慢緣有漏一分可意事生，恚緣一分非可意生，是故此三煩惱一分所生，名取一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又貪與慢這二種煩惱是緣著有漏的一部分可意事而產生的，恚是緣一部分不可意事所生。凡夫於可意境，容易生喜、生樂產生貪著，於自己或自己所擁有的可意境洋洋得意而生慢；於不如意境，常常暴怒不安，總想快快脫離而生瞋恚。這三種煩惱都是因一部分的狀況而產生，因此稱為取一分事為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、取一切事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科取一切事，說明煩惱取一切事為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4718"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所餘煩惱，通緣內外若愛非愛，及俱相違有漏事生，是故說彼名曰遍行，取一切事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除貪、慢與恚所餘的七種煩惱，遍緣一切內身、外境，可愛的、不可愛的，或是可愛不可愛俱非的有漏事而生，所以稱為遍行，取一切事為所緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又十煩惱等者：如下分別：煩惱，幾有事？幾無事？謂諸見與慢是無事，於諸行中實無有我而分別轉故。貪、恚是有事。無明、疑通二種。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/59.htm#46734:47588">陵本五十九卷三頁4792</a>）今於此中麤相建立，總說一切煩惱，見所斷者，名曰無事。所餘煩惱修所斷者，應名有事，不通無事，相相違故，非由分別起故。如下自說：見、修所斷諸漏煩惱，當知略有五種所緣。一、緣邪分別所起事境，二、緣見境，三、緣戒禁境，四、緣自分別所起名境，五、緣任運堅固事境。當知此中，前四所緣皆非成實，故彼煩惱名曰無事。第五所緣其相相違，以彼修所斷漏，緣自任運堅固事境，由是因緣，應名有事。文說無事，其義難通，疑是衍文。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如下文還會分別：煩惱，哪些是有事？哪些是無事？思想上的種種見，及高慢心是屬於無事，在有為法當中沒有真實的我，但有情的分別心卻認為有這回事，所以是無事。貪恚是有事，通常是因為由真實的境界而引起的。無明及懷疑這二種煩惱是通於有事無事，在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷59，1950頁還會說到。這裡是麤相建立，總說一切煩惱，若是見道所斷的煩惱稱為無事，所餘修所斷的煩惱應稱為有事，因為它的相狀與見道所斷的煩惱不一樣，它是俱生起的，不是分別起的，不應通於無事。如下文說：見、修所斷煩惱，當知要略而言有五種所緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、錯誤的分別所現起的事境；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、思想上的境界；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、緣身語的戒禁境；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、緣內心的分別所起的名境，有這樣的名字（能詮）就現出那樣的境（所詮）。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、緣五蘊，或者是器世間，這種是任運的，而且是堅固的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道這五種當中，前四種所緣境都不是真實的因緣所生法，所以它不是真實，這一類的煩惱稱為無事，第五種所緣境界的相貌與前四種所緣境相違反，因為它是修所斷的有漏煩惱，緣俱生的、真實的種種因緣所生事境而生起，應該說所餘煩惱是有事。此處既然說彼相違故，所餘煩惱，應該說有事，才與上文所說：「見所斷者名曰無事」相反，現在又將有事無事放在一起說，它的義理很難通達，所以懷疑是多出來的文。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、隨煩惱差別2　卯一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨煩惱差別，解釋隨煩惱差別，分二科；第一科總標，總相標出隨煩惱的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有隨順如是煩惱、煩惱俱行、煩惱品類，名隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若有隨順如上所說十種煩惱，又與煩惱一起活動，屬於十種煩惱的種類，這種隨著根本煩惱生起的煩惱，稱為隨煩惱。 若據下文所說，隨順如是煩惱，包括根本煩惱及大中小隨煩惱，煩惱俱行是說明十種根本煩惱是否相應俱行的情形，煩惱品類說明小隨煩惱是根本煩惱的品類。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　卷8說：倒染心故，名隨煩惱。煩惱顛倒染汙有情的心，名為隨煩惱。隨煩惱是根本煩惱的異名。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷16：窺基大師說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、隨順是總句，或尋伺睡眠等體性不是煩惱隨順根本煩惱，故名煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、或謂別境心所中數與煩惱煩惱俱行者，指隨煩惱由四相俱行故，名隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、煩惱品類者即忿恨等小隨煩惱，如下文是諸品類等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　也有另一種解釋：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、隨順如是煩惱是總句。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、煩惱俱行者，指無漸無愧等二十二法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、煩惱品類者，指尋伺悔眠。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有解釋：中隨煩惱大隨煩惱二類煩惱名煩惱俱行，十種小隨煩惱名煩惱品類。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在解釋：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、隨順煩惱者總標。隨煩惱名通攝尋伺悔眠。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、煩惱俱行者，指中隨煩惱大隨煩惱二類。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、煩惱品類者，顯示十種小隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、別釋3　辰一、隨順煩惱攝2　巳一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別解釋隨煩惱，分三科；第一科隨順煩惱攝，說明隨順煩惱所攝，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名隨煩惱？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為隨煩惱？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋2　午一、明建立2　未一、顯差別2　申一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋隨煩惱的體性，分二科；第一科明建立，說明隨煩惱的建立，又分二科；第一科顯差別，顯示隨煩惱的差別相，又分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出隨煩惱相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4719"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">略由四相差別建立。一、通一切不善心起；二、通一切染汙心起；三、於各別不善心起；四、善、不善、無記心起，非一切處、非一切時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要略而言隨煩惱由四相差別建立：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、遍一切不善心都有這種煩惱；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、一切染汙心生起時才有，染汙心指有覆無記心；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、依各別不善心而生起；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、通於善、不善、無記心生起，不是三界一切處都能生起、也不是一切時相續生起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《百法明門論論義》卷1說：「隨」有三義。一、指自類俱起，自已這一類的隨煩惱生起；二、遍不善性，指遍於一切不善心時都有這種隨煩惱；三、遍諸染心，指遍於一切染汙心時都有這種隨煩惱。具足三種特性稱為大隨煩惱；具足二種特性稱為中隨煩惱；不具足三種，於不善心中各別而生起者，稱為小隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》非一切處非一切時者：如下自釋：尋伺乃至初靜慮地。惡作、睡眠唯在欲界。由是說言非一切處。非去來今定相續轉，由是說言非一切時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如下文解釋：尋伺的現行在欲界乃至初靜慮地。惡作（後悔）心所及睡眠心所只發生在欲界，所以說有些隨煩惱心所並不是一切處生起。而且有些隨煩惱心所也不是過去、現在、未來都相續生起，因此說有些隨煩惱心所並不是一切時生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、隨釋2　酉一、不定地攝4　戌一、通一切不善心起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分二科；第一科不定地攝，說明不定地所攝隨煩惱，又分四科；第一科通一切不善心起，說明通一切不善心起的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂無慚、無愧，名通一切不善心起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無慚、無愧這二種隨煩惱，在一切不善心生起時，都同時一起相應而轉，也因為有無慚無愧，才會生起貪瞋癡等煩惱。這二種隨煩惱，發生作用的範圍比大隨煩惱小，具足自類俱起及遍不善性二種隨義，但只遍不善性，不通有覆的情形，又稱為中隨煩惱，屬於欲界沒有禪定、不定地所攝的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、通一切染汙心起2　亥一、出體</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科通一切染汙心起，說明通一切染汙心起的隨煩惱，分二科；第一科出體，說明這些隨煩惱的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">隨煩惱放逸、掉舉、惛沈、不信、懈怠、邪欲、邪勝解、邪念、散亂、不正知，此十隨煩惱，通一切染汙心起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨煩惱：放逸、掉舉、惛沈、不信、懈怠、邪欲、邪勝解、邪念、散亂、不正知這十種隨煩惱，通一切染汙心，都會生起。放逸等十種隨煩惱，因為具足自類俱起、遍不善性、及遍諸染心三種隨義，染汙的有漏心生時，都能生起這種隨煩惱，又稱為大隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、明繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明繫，說明十種大隨煩惱的界地所繫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4720"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">通一切處三界所繫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三界都是染汙有漏，因此十種大隨煩惱通三界一切處起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、各別不善心起2　亥一、辨體相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科各別不善心起，說明各別不善心起的隨煩惱，分二科；第一科辨體相，辨明小隨煩惱各別不善心起的體性相貌。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂、憍、害，此十隨煩惱，各別不善心起。若一生時，必無第二。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　忿、恨、覆、惱、嫉、慳、誑、諂、憍、害，這十種隨煩惱，行相麤猛，各別不善心起，各自為主。一個「忿」心生起，就沒有其餘小隨煩惱可同時生起，不具足三種義稱為小隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、明界繫2　天一、出唯欲界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明界繫，說明小隨煩惱的界繫，分二科；第一科出唯欲界，說出唯欲界繫的隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是十種，皆欲界繫，除誑、諂、憍。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是這十種小隨煩惱，都是繫屬欲界的煩惱，除了誑、諂、憍，是通於三界，下文還要各別說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、簡所說餘</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡所說餘，簡別其餘三種小隨煩惱界繫差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由誑及諂至初靜慮。憍通三界，此并前二，若在上地，唯無記性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欺騙、諂媚，通常是與名聞利養有關係，因此說誑及諂只到初靜慮及初靜慮以下。於自盛事心生醉傲為憍，通於三界。憍與前面誑、諂二種煩惱，如果是在上地，色、無色界天，由奢摩他所制伏的緣故，是屬於無記性，但是它障礙聖道，所以是有覆的，合稱有覆無記。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此并前二等者：義顯憍及誑、諂，在欲界繫，不善心起；若在上地，性唯無記。由奢摩他力所執持故，多白淨法所攝受故，義如前說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡說并前二等，義理上顯示憍及前二的誑、諂是屬欲界繫的不善心起；如果在上二地的色界、無色界，它們的體性是無記的。因為有定的力量制伏，多分是善法所攝受，它的義理如同前面所說。上二地有情雖然也會有煩惱，但是屬於無記性的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、通善不善無記心起2　亥一、出體性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科通善不善無記心起，說明通三性心起的隨煩惱，分二科；第一科出體性，說出通三性心起的隨煩惱體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">尋、伺、惡作、睡眠，此四隨煩惱，通善、不善、無記心起，非一切處、非一切時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　尋、伺、惡作及睡眠，這四種隨煩惱，通於善心、不善心、無記心中，都會生起。但是它不是遍三界一切處生，也不是一切時相續生起。惡作，是後悔已做的善事或惡事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4721"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、別明繫2　天一、尋伺</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別明繫，辨別說明不定心所的界繫差別，分二科；第一科尋伺，說明尋伺心所的界繫差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有極久尋求伺察，便令身疲、念失，心亦勞損，是故尋、伺名隨煩惱。此二乃至初靜慮地。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果有人很長時間尋求所知事，於所知事作粗的思惟觀察，或作細的思惟觀察，便使令身體疲勞、念力忘失，心也勞累受損，所以尋、伺稱為隨煩惱。此二種隨煩惱，欲界眾生乃至到初靜慮地都有。智者大師說：覺觀（即尋伺）過盛，妨礙坐禪。一切法唯識所現，可見病也是由心所生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從前有一人生重病纏綿床褥多年，已經到了奄奄一息，百藥罔效了。這時剛好有一位高僧路過他家，就為他開示說：你的病都是由煩惱所生，煩惱由妄想而來。妄想有三種：一、追憶數十年來榮枯恩怨及種種閒事，這是回想過去的妄想；二、事到眼前，可以順應，卻強生意見，猶豫不決，這是現在的妄想；三、期望日後富貴如願，子孫光耀門楣及不一定能成、能得的事，這是未來的妄想。這三種妄想忽生忽滅，念念不停，佛教說這是幻心；若能反觀自照，知道全是妄想，知幻即離，自然就消滅了，離幻即覺，佛教說這是覺心。所以說：不怕念起，只怕覺遲，念起是病，不續是藥。又告訴他說：你的病也是水、火不交所生，若是外貪女色，這是外感之欲，若是夜思佳麗，這是內生之欲，若染著這內外二欲，耗散元氣，如果能夠斷除，則腎水自然滋生，可以上交於心。至於思索文字，廢寢忘食，這是理障；經營職業，不怕辛勞，這是事障。這二種雖然不是色欲，若毫無節制，也是損害性靈。若能減緩，則心火不會上升，可以下交於腎。若是水火相濟，病自然就好了。病人聽完，就依教奉行，獨處一室，掃空萬緣，攝心靜坐，坐到一個多月，病就漸漸好了。由此可見尋、伺五欲、道理或俗事過多時，都會損害身心，障礙修習止觀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、悔眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科悔眠，說明悔眠心所的界繫差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">惡作、睡眠唯在欲界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　惡作、睡眠這二種隨煩惱，只有在欲界才有。惡作，是心追悔過去所做，於過去所做善、惡事都可能生起追悔之心，上二界眾生不會有這種追悔之心，所以沒有惡作心所，有禪定，不用睡覺，所以沒有睡眠；欲界眾生如果有禪定的，通常睡眠也會很少。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、定地攝2　戌一、出體</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科定地攝，說明定地所攝的隨煩惱，分二科；第一科出體，說出定地所攝隨煩惱的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有定地諸隨煩惱。謂尋、伺、誑、諂、惛沈、掉舉、憍、放逸、懈怠等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又得到禪定的人，還有尋、伺、誑、諂、惛沈、掉舉、憍、放逸、懈怠等隨煩惱。這些煩惱，隨時都會干擾得到禪定的人，比如得定之後懈怠，就不能往上升進了。這其中誑、諂、憍是小隨煩惱，尋、伺是不定心所，惛沈、掉舉、放逸、懈怠等是中隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、明繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明繫，說明定地所攝隨煩惱的界繫差別。</span></span></span></div>
