<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、了知煩惱的自性過患，要知道煩惱的體性有很多過失災患，才能生起出離心。〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8說：諸煩惱有無量過患。因為煩惱現行時，先惱亂有情的內心，其次於所緣境發起顛倒，令諸煩惱種子更加堅固，令煩惱等流相續而行；能引發對自己的傷害，能引發對他人的傷害，能引發對自己與他人的傷害；能生現在生命體的罪過，能生當來生命體的罪過，能同時生現在與當來生命體的罪過，使令有情領受罪過所生的身心憂苦，能引生老病死等種種大苦；能令相續的生命遠離涅槃的勝義樂；能令退失種種殊勝的善法；能令資具財富衰敗、損害、散失；能令入眾不得無畏、悚懼、沒有威德；能令惡名昭彰，流布十方；常為有智慧的人之所訶斥詆毀；令臨終時生大憂苦後悔；令身壞已後墮到惡趣，到地獄受苦；令不能證得自己殊勝的出世間利益等，煩惱的過失災患實在無量無邊。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、思惟對治所緣境相，知道煩惱有無量無邊的過失災患後，應該要思惟怎麼對治煩惱的凈行所緣境相。比如貪欲多的人，於所緣境相多取淨妙相，因此必須思惟所緣境相不淨才能加以對治。〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷26，901頁起說到五種淨行所緣，就是此處所說思惟對治所緣境相，能令行者調伏煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》思惟對治所緣境相者：本地分中聲聞地說：淨行所緣，謂不淨、慈愍、緣性緣起、界差別、阿那波那念等所緣差別。如彼廣釋應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/26.htm#46907:22103">陵本二十六卷十九頁2228</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷26，909頁說了很多修行的道理。淨行所緣，淨是指清淨，行，是指心，清淨內心煩惱的所緣境，稱為淨行所緣。根據眾生的根性不同，有五種，天臺宗稱為五停心觀：包括不淨、慈愍、緣性緣起、界差別、阿那波那念等所緣差別，如〈聲聞地〉詳細解釋應知。要略而言，貪欲重的眾生，應該常常思惟不淨的所緣，調伏貪欲的煩惱。心比較剛強容易生氣的人，應該修慈悲觀，慈愍觀就是慈悲觀。愚癡的眾生，不明白因果道理的人，應該修緣性緣起，緣性是指四緣（因緣、等無間緣、所緣緣、增上緣），緣起是指十二緣起，思惟這些道理可以對治於因果的愚癡及生死輪轉的愚癡。觀察身體由地水火風空識六種因所組成，無我可得，修界差別觀，可以對治因我執而生的高慢心。修阿那波那念所緣，又名數息觀，可以對治散亂心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、以勝善品滋心相續。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、以勝善品滋心相續。勝善品，殊勝的善品，最主要是修止觀或是念佛、參禪、種種的法門，應當修施戒忍等殊勝的善品，滋養內心，而且必須相續，要有恒心，每天、每個小時、每個剎那，都是這樣子不斷地努力思惟對治所緣境相，才能對治煩惱纏。披尋記說勝善品是指二道資糧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此是永斷正見前行之道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　當知這是永斷煩惱，得到無漏正見的前行之道，前方便。這還只是前方便而已，只是調伏煩惱的現行，唯有將煩惱種子全部斷除，才是真正的無漏正見。《瑜伽論記》說，前面二種是在資糧位，後一種是在加行位。第一、二種了知煩惱自性過患，及思惟對治所緣境相，是屬於資糧位的行者所應該做到的。第三種是修止觀，屬於加行位的，至少有未到地定，能在定中修觀，開始漸漸斷除煩惱，但是還沒有永斷，只是伏住它而已。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4735"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》以勝善品滋心相續者：本地分中聲聞地說：護養定資糧處，成就戒律儀等一切善法差別。其義應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/30.htm#46913:25067">陵本三十卷五頁2499</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧聲聞地〉說：護養定資糧處，成就戒律儀等一切善法差別。這些道理應當了知。在〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷30，1001頁說了十四種定資糧：自、他圓滿、善法欲；戒、根律儀、食知量；悎寤、正知住、善友；聞、思、無障、捨、莊嚴，這些定資糧都是修行人應當具足的，這還是在加行位，是伏煩惱攝。伏煩惱要做到這三件事情，一、了知煩惱自性過患，二、思惟對治所緣境相，三、以勝善品滋心相續者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、斷煩惱攝2　辰一、約種類辨2　巳一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科斷煩惱攝，說明斷煩惱所攝，分二科；第一科約種類辨，約斷煩惱的種類分辨，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸修行者斷煩惱時，為捨纏耶？捨隨眠耶？由斷何故，說名為斷？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：諸多修行人斷煩惱時，是捨掉煩惱的現行？還是捨掉煩惱的種子？到底是斷現行還是斷種子，才稱為斷？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、答3　午一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科標，標出斷煩惱種子，說名為斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：但捨隨眠。以煩惱纏先已捨故。斷隨眠故，說名為斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：棄捨煩惱的種子，才稱為斷煩惱。因為煩惱的現行，在修勝善品滋心相續的時候，已經捨棄了。因此斷煩惱種子，才說名為斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">雖纏已斷，未斷隨眠，諸煩惱纏數復現起；若隨眠斷，纏與隨眠畢竟不起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼斷煩惱的種子才稱為斷？因為雖然煩惱的現行已經斷了，可是沒有斷掉煩惱種子，斬草未除根，春風吹又生；煩惱的種子，現在沒有生起現行，不表示沒有煩惱，只要有境界時還是會數數現起；如果煩惱的種子斷除了，煩惱的現行就永遠不會現起。斷除煩惱猶如拔草，如果拔草只拔表面，一下雨就長得更快。古代禪師說：出門便是草，當煩惱的種子尚未斷除，門是指眼耳鼻舌身意，六根只要一出去緣取色等六境界，就是煩惱，稱為草，此時如草的煩惱就順理成章長出來了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、約三世辨2　巳一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約三世辨，約過去未來現在辨明斷煩惱差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：為斷過去？為斷未來？為斷現在？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：斷煩惱時是斷過去的煩惱種子？是斷未來的煩惱種子？還是斷現在的煩惱種子？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、答3　午一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科標，標出非斷及斷的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4736"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：非斷去來今，然說斷三世。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：事實上斷煩惱種子，不是斷過去、現在、未來的煩惱種子，然而假名安立說是斷三世的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼原因？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、釋2　未一、非斷去來今3　申一、非過去</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科非斷去來今，說明不是斷三世煩惱，又分三科；第一科非過去，說明不是斷過去煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若在過去有隨眠心，任運滅故，其性已斷，復何所斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果在過去，有煩惱種子的那一念心，任運自然滅了，它的體性已經沒有了，還斷什麼煩惱種子？這是解釋非斷過去。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、非未來</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科非未來，說明不是斷未來的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若在未來有隨眠心，性未生故，體既是無，當何所斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果是在未來，有煩惱種子的那一念心，還沒有產生，它的體性還沒有，要斷什麼？所以也不是斷未來的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、非現在2　酉一、由剎那不住</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科非現在，說明不是斷現在煩惱種子，分二科；第一科由剎那不住，第一種情況，由現在煩惱種子由剎那不住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若在現在有隨眠心，此剎那後，性必不住，更何須斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果說是斷現在的煩惱種子，有煩惱種子的那一念心，剎那以後，它的體性也不會安住，又何須斷。〈本地分‧思所成地〉說：「諸行皆剎那，住尚無況用，即說彼生起，為用為作者。」煩惱現起以後，這個煩惱體性也不會一直住下去，剎那生、剎那滅，如幻如化，了無實體，又何須斷掉煩惱的種子？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、由不和合起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由不和合起，第二種情況，由煩惱種子與能對治的清淨心不和合起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4737"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有隨眠離隨眠心二不和合，是故現在亦非所斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有煩惱種子的心，及離煩惱種子的心：一念能對治煩惱種子的清淨心，證得無分別智的時候，名離隨眠心，這二種體性是不一樣的，不能和合，所以也不是斷現在的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、說斷去來今2　申一、舉道理</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科說斷去來今，說明如何斷三世煩惱，分二科；第一科舉道理，說明斷三世煩惱種子的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">然從他音、內正作意二因緣故，正見相應。隨所治惑，能治心生，諸有隨眠所治心滅。此心生時，彼心滅時，平等平等，對治生滅道理應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說不是斷去來今，可是又說斷三世，怎麼說是斷三世？然而從聽聞佛所說的法及內心能正確的如理作意，這二種因緣的緣故，能有正確的見地、與諸法實相相應的正見產生。隨所對治的煩惱，能對治的智心產生時，攝持隨眠之所對治的識心就滅了。這一念正見相應的心生時，也是無分別智產生時，正是被對治的攝持煩惱種子的識消滅時，如秤之兩頭，低昂時等，能治的智慧產生與所治隨眠的消滅是同時的，稱為平等平等。對治生滅的道理應該知道也是這樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋彼斷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋彼斷，解釋斷三世煩惱種子的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">正見相應能對治心，於現在世無有隨眠，於過去世亦無隨眠；此剎那後離隨眠心，在未來世亦無隨眠。從此已後，於已轉依、已斷隨眠身相續中，所有後得世間所攝善、無記心去來今位，皆離隨眠，是故三世皆得說斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果有正見相應能對治的心，與煩惱種子是不能同時存在的，所以在現在世沒有煩惱的種子，過去也沒有煩惱種子；正見能對治心相應後，下一剎那未來世，也沒有煩惱的種子。從正見相應能對治的心初斷煩惱種子以後，展轉精進，證無學果，於已經轉變的所依心（阿賴耶識轉成異熟識）、已斷除煩惱種子的色受想行識當中，所有的後得智所攝世間善心、無記心，過去現在未來都沒有煩惱的種子，此時善、無記心都是無漏的，因此可以說是斷過去、現在、未來的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結說名煩惱雜染染淨差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名煩惱雜染染淨差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這就是煩惱雜染與清淨的差別。斷煩惱種子才名為斷，根據勝義的道理斷煩惱種子不是斷三世的煩惱種子，但是根據世俗諦，後得智所攝世間善心、無記心而說是斷三世的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》從此已後等者：前說正見相應能對治心，有學位攝。從此已後，證無學果，名已轉依，一切煩惱隨眠已斷。彼相續中，世間所攝善法、若無記法諸相應心去來今位，不為一切世間增上種子之所隨逐，名離隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說正見相應能對治心，屬有學位所攝。從此之後，展轉精進，證阿羅漢果，稱為已轉依，將阿賴耶識中所有的愛見煩惱種子斷除。阿羅漢在所餘生命相續中，行於世間所攝的善法、或無記法時諸相應的心在過去、未來、現在，不再為能生一切世間果報的煩惱種子之所隨逐，名為離隨眠。因為阿羅漢沒有煩惱的種子，所做的都是善法或無記法，不會再去招感世間的生死果報，稱為離隨眠。這段文將調伏煩惱和斷煩惱說得很清楚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、迷斷差別2　丑一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科迷斷差別，說明煩惱雜染的迷惑與斷除的差別，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何建立煩惱雜染迷斷差別？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如何建立煩惱雜染的迷惑與斷除的差別？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、釋2　寅一、略說2　卯一、舉所斷2　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科略說，要略說明煩惱雜染的迷斷，又分二科；第一科舉所斷，舉出所斷的煩惱，又分二科；第一科標，標出所斷的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4738"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知略說有十五種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道所斷的煩惱，要略歸納起來有十五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋2　巳一、舉欲界繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉欲界繫，舉出繫屬於欲界的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂欲界繫，見苦集滅道諦所斷，及修所斷，諸漏有五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　包括現在世煩惱及煩惱的種子，都稱為繫。屬於欲界繫的煩惱與煩惱種子，是見道位證得苦集滅道四諦時所斷的煩惱與修道位時所要斷除的煩惱，總合見道及修道所要斷除的煩惱一共有五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、例色無色等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例色無色等，說明色界與無色界的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如欲界繫，色無色繫各五亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如見道位與修道位所斷的欲界繫煩惱一共有五種，色界繫與無色界繫的煩惱，也各別有五種，加起來共有十五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知略說有十五種等者：三界諸漏見斷、修斷，各說有五。謂依四諦，見斷分四，於修斷中總說為一，是故說五。如是三界有十五種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三界的煩惱，屬於見所斷和修所斷各有五種；依迷於苦集滅道四諦而言，見道所斷分別起的煩惱有四種，修道所斷俱生起的煩惱總說有一種，合有五種。如是三界共有十五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、列迷諦2　辰一、欲界攝2　巳一、迷苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列迷諦，列出眾生對四諦迷惑的煩惱，分二科；第一科欲界攝，說明欲界所攝的情況，又分二科；第一科迷苦，迷於欲界苦諦的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲界迷苦有十煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色受想行識五蘊就是苦，欲界凡夫有情迷於苦諦有十種根本煩惱產生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、迷集等2　午一、舉迷集</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科迷集等，迷於欲界集諦等的煩惱，分二科；第一科舉迷集，舉出迷於欲界集諦的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">迷集有八，除薩迦耶及邊執見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　迷於欲界集諦的煩惱有八種，除了薩迦耶及邊執見以外，包括邪見、見取見、戒禁取見、貪、恚、慢、無明和疑。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4739"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例迷滅道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例迷滅道，例舉迷滅諦、道諦的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如迷集諦，滅、道亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如迷於集諦的煩惱有八種，迷於欲界滅諦、道諦也一樣，各有八種。《瑜伽論記》卷16解釋這段文說：欲界迷苦有十種煩惱，迷餘三諦各有八種煩惱除身、邊見；上界除瞋，餘如後說。〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8及下文廣辨處說：欲界四諦所斷各有十種煩惱；上二界除瞋。欲界修所斷煩惱有六種，上二界除瞋各五種。為什麼前後兩段文所說不同？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三藏法師說：斷煩惱有二種說法。一、迷諦起惑門，諸諦都有十種所斷煩惱，這是大乘所說。二、諦行斷惑門，如苦諦下有空行、無我行，為能對治，有身見為所對治；既有無常行為能治，就有邊見執常為所對治，因此說苦諦下具十種煩惱，餘諦沒有這能治之道，也就是沒有所對治身、邊二見，因此餘諦所斷煩惱僅各有八種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　窺基大師說，見、修二種所斷煩惱依經論有三種說法：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、苦諦下有十種煩惱，集滅諦下有七種煩惱，道諦下有八種煩惱，這種如薩婆多部《俱舍論》等所說；龍樹菩薩隨此門故說有九十八使（欲界有貪瞋癡慢四種思惑，色界、無色界各有貪癡慢三種思惑，三界思惑，共為十使，并前見惑八十八使，合之而為九十八）。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、苦諦下有十，三諦各有八種煩惱，此說如經部等所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、四諦下各有十種煩惱，這是大乘真實道理，唯識所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《雜集論》卷7說：苦、集二諦是十種煩惱之因緣，增長這十種煩惱，又為十種煩惱之依止處，性能隨順生這十種煩惱。這種說法與本論卷8所說相同。窺基大師《成唯識論述記》卷6說到迷四諦有總迷別迷的差別：於見道迷諦煩惱，有總有別。總迷是指十種煩惱都通迷四諦，即一一煩惱皆起之時，迷四諦理。又諸煩惱有各別行相，名別迷四諦，如哪一種煩惱是迷苦諦等，這是其中一諦下各別的煩惱行相，隨於此諦下生見、疑之後而生這種煩惱，就說這種煩惱是迷這一諦。總迷四諦有二種。一數總，四諦各具十種煩惱；二行相總，有通迷四諦故。別迷四諦也有二種。一數別，三諦有八種煩惱，一諦有十種煩惱；二行相別，各各別迷故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、上界攝2　巳一、顯別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科上界攝，說明色界和無色界所攝迷於四諦的煩惱，分二科；第一科顯別，顯示與欲界有差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">上界諸諦并除瞋恚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色、無色界因為得到禪定以後就沒有瞋心了，除掉瞋煩惱，只有七種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、例同</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例同，上二界迷於四諦的次第如同欲界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">隨迷次第，如欲界說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　上二界迷於四諦的次第，如欲界一樣。迷於苦諦有九種，迷於集諦有七種，滅諦、道諦也各有七種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》隨迷次第如欲界說者：隨四諦別，有四迷執，名迷次第。迷相是一，說如欲界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨苦、集、滅、道四諦的分別，有四種迷執，名為迷的次第。色、無色界有情迷於四諦的行相和欲界一樣，所以說如欲界，除了瞋以外。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、廣辨2　卯一、辨差別2　辰一、辨2　巳一、見斷攝4　午一、迷苦2　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣辨，詳細辨別煩惱迷斷差別，分二科；第一科辨差別，說明煩惱迷斷的差別，又分二科；第一科辨，分辨差別，又分二科；第一科見斷攝，見道所斷、所攝的煩惱差別，又分四科；第一科迷苦，迷於苦諦的煩惱，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何迷苦有十隨眠？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼說迷於苦諦有十種煩惱種子？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋2　申一、別辨10　酉一、由薩迦耶見</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科別辨，各別說明這十種煩惱，又分二科；第一科由薩迦耶見，由迷於苦諦生我見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">略五取蘊總名為苦。愚夫於此五取蘊中，起二十句薩迦耶見。五句見我，餘見我所。是名迷苦薩迦耶見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　凡夫五蘊由煩惱愛取而得，名五取蘊。要略而言五取蘊總稱為苦。愚痴無聞凡夫對於色、受、想、行、識五取蘊生起二十種我見，其中有五句是我見，其他的見是執著五蘊為我所有的我所見，這些總稱迷苦薩迦耶見。苦是指五蘊，對於五蘊有迷惑，生起我見及我所見，稱為迷苦諦，這是煩惱的根源。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4740"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》五句見我餘見我所者：集論中說：於五取蘊，有二十句薩迦耶見。謂計色是我，我有諸色，色屬於我，我在色中；如是計受、想、行、識是我，我有識等，識等屬我，我在識等中。於此諸見，幾是我見？幾是我所見？謂五是我見，十五是我所見。何因十五是我所見？由相應我所故，隨轉我所故，不離我所故。（集論一卷八頁）此應準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《集論》中說：於五取蘊，有二十句薩迦耶見。是指執著色身是我、我有種種色、色身屬於我、我住在色身中；如是執著感受、思想、行（意志、造作）、識（能了別的心）是我；我有種種受、想、行、識；受、想、行、識屬於我；或我住在受、想、行、識中也是一樣。在這些見當中，哪些是我見？哪些是我所見？若是執著色、受、想、行、識是我，這五句屬於我見，這是執著「即蘊是我」；若是執著我有種種色乃至識，色身乃至識屬於我，或我住在色身中乃至識中，這十五句屬於我所見，這是執著「離蘊有我」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼說這十五句是我所見？若執著我有諸色乃至識，是因為執著離蘊有我，離開色受想行識，另外有一個我單獨存在，那個我和色乃至識相應，一起合作做事，色乃至識是屬於我所有的，所以說我有諸色乃至識，這是由相應我所故，屬於我所見。若執著色身乃至識屬於我，是指執著色身乃至識能隨我的意志而轉，我要不要走路、活動、說話、做事，是我可以主宰的；乃至我要不要了別境界，也隨我的意志而轉。世間人都說這個身體是我的，這是我的感受、我覺得痛苦或我覺得快樂；這是我的想法，我認為這件事好或壞等；這是我的意志，我的決定操之在我；這是我的心，我的心想做什麼事等，諸如此類色身乃至識隨我而轉，所以說色屬於我，這是由隨轉我所故，屬於我所見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若執著我住在色身中乃至識中，執著獨立存在的我、離蘊的我，住在色乃至識，有的人執著離蘊的我很小，像一粒豆子，有的人執著離蘊的我很大，周遍十方，這是執著色乃至識屬於我所有，這是由不離我所故，屬於我所見。這是《集論》卷1，8頁所說，此處應準照《集論》所說可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、由邊執見</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由邊執見，由迷於苦諦生邊執見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即用如是薩迦耶見以為依止，於五取蘊見我斷常，故邊執見亦迷於苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又用以上所說於五蘊所生薩迦耶見（包含我見及我所見）為依止，在五取蘊上取著斷見、常見，所以邊執見也是迷於苦諦而生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、由邪見6　戌一、謗無因等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由邪見，說明由邪見而謗無因等，分六科；第一科謗無因等，由迷於苦諦，生起毀謗沒有因、果等邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又諸邪見，謂無施等，乃至妙行、惡行業果及與異熟，是迷苦諦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又迷於苦諦的邪見，是指毀謗沒有布施，乃至妙行、惡行的業果及感得異熟果報，這是迷於苦諦而生的邪見。沒有善惡因果觀念，這就是邪見。這種邪見是依於苦諦，依於色受想行識而生起的，稱為迷苦諦的邪見。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、謗無父母等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科謗無父母等，由迷於苦諦，毀謗沒有父母等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有邪見，撥無父母、化生有情，如是邪見一分迷苦、一分迷集。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種邪見，誹謗沒有父母或沒有化生有情，這些撥無父母及化生有情（中有）的邪見，一部分是迷於苦諦，一部分是迷於集諦而生。父母本身的體性就是一種苦，因為是一種果報體，也是色受想行識，所以說是迷苦；如果就父母能夠生孩子而言，這是因，從父母是生男女的因地說是迷於集諦。化生有情本身也是一種苦，因為也是一種果報體，也是色受想行識，所以說是迷於苦諦；又化生有情能感生後有業之因，也是迷於於集諦。因此若是撥無父母、撥無化生有情的邪見，一分迷於苦諦，一分迷於集諦而生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、謗苦諦法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科謗苦諦法，說明由迷於苦諦，毀謗苦諦法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="50995:46982"></a>又諸外道誹謗苦諦，起大邪見。彼謂沙門喬答摩種，為諸弟子施設苦諦，此定無有。如是邪見亦迷苦諦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦是指色受想行識五取蘊，這件事情是真實的，只有聖人才知道五取蘊真實是苦，外道卻誹謗苦諦這件事，生起大邪見。他們認為沙門喬答摩種（梵語，義譯牛糞種、或甘蔗種、泥土種，古譯瞿曇），是指釋迦牟尼佛，為諸弟子們施設安立苦諦，決定沒有這件事，這樣的邪見也是迷於苦諦所生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4741"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、計自在等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科計自在等，由迷於苦諦，虛妄計執自在天等常住不變，是第四種邪見執著。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有諸見，妄計自在、世主、釋、梵及餘物類，為常、為恆，無有變易。如是邪見亦迷苦諦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種邪見，虛妄計執他化自在天、世間的主宰者、帝釋、梵天王、及其他種類的世間主宰者，執著這些創世者與主宰者是常住、恆久、沒有變化改易的。這些邪見也是迷於苦諦所生。不能了知即使是天人，他們的五取蘊也是無常、苦、空、無我。世主，是指色界第四禪最高天，摩醯首羅天，以果報最殊勝，居色界頂，能覆蓋三千大千世界，為世間的主宰者。釋，指帝釋，釋提桓因。梵，指大梵天王。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌五、計邊無邊</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科計邊無邊，由迷於苦諦，虛妄計執有邊或無邊等邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有諸見計邊、無邊，如是亦名迷苦邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種邪見，虛妄計執世間及有情是有邊或無邊，這類邪見也是迷於苦諦所生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌六、不死矯亂一分</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科不死矯亂一分，說明不死矯亂的一部分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有沙門、若婆羅門不死矯亂邪見一分，亦迷苦諦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有出家沙門或者是在家有學問的婆羅門，有一分不死矯亂的邪見，這也是迷於苦諦而生的邪見。不死矯亂詳細內容如前文所說，不死是指天，外道求生天，卻不知道真正的生天之道，又認為能夠沒有錯誤的回答不亂問者的話，即可生天。但是這類人實在不懂，也沒有學習佛法，既擔心他人知道自己不懂，又擔心回答他人的問題不正確時不能生天，因此若有人來問有關不死天的情形時，卻矯亂而答。這類人是不了解不死天的五蘊，也是無常、苦、空、無我，而妄求生天所產生的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、由見取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科由見取，由迷於苦諦生見取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有見取，妄取迷苦所有諸見以為第一，謂能清淨、解脫、出離，如是名為迷苦見取。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若有見取，虛妄計執迷於五取蘊的種種邪見，包括前面所說的薩迦耶見、邊執見、或者邪見等，是最正確、最好、最第一、最殊勝的，能夠使自己內心清淨、解脫煩惱、出離生死，這都是因為迷於五取蘊的邪見而產生見取，名為迷苦的見取。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉五、由戒禁取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科由戒禁取，由迷於苦諦生戒禁取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有妄取隨順此見，此見隨法所受戒禁，以為第一，能得清淨、解脫、出離，此戒禁取，是迷苦諦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果妄取種種邪見，隨順見取，配合見取所受的身護、語護等戒律，禁止不可以做這件事，不可以做那件事，或者持牛戒、持狗戒，執著這些不合法、錯誤的身護、語護，能夠使自己內心清淨、解脫煩惱、出離生死，這些戒禁取都是因為迷於苦諦所生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4742"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉六、由疑</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科由疑，由迷於苦諦生疑。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有外道於此諸見不定信受，亦不一向誹謗如來所立苦諦，但於苦諦心懷猶豫，此及所餘於苦猶豫，是迷苦疑。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若有外道對種種的薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見、見取見、戒禁取見等，不一定相信接受，也不是完全誹謗佛所安立的苦諦：色受想行識是苦。可是對於苦諦心懷猶豫，心想五蘊真的是苦嗎？關於這些或其他種種苦，心懷猶豫，這類是迷於苦諦所生的疑。懷疑五蘊是否是苦的心情，不一定是外道，現在周圍的人可能就有這種想法，若告訴這類人五蘊是苦，對方哪裡知道是苦？這類人家庭美滿，覺得很快樂，怎麼說苦？也是會懷疑的。知苦是聖人的智慧，實非一般凡夫所能理解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉七、由貪</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科由貪，由迷於苦諦生貪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於如是自所起見寶愛堅著，如此見貪，是迷苦貪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果對自己於五蘊所生起的種種錯誤思想、見解，很寶貴、愛著並且堅固執著，這種思想上的貪，是迷於苦諦所生，稱為迷苦貪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉八、由恚</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科由恚，由迷於苦諦生恚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於異分他所起見，心懷違損，是迷苦恚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果對於他人不同於自己的見解，心想要違背、損害他，這是迷於苦諦所生諸見引生的瞋恚，稱為迷苦恚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉九、由慢</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科由慢，由迷於苦諦生慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若恃此見，心生高舉，是迷苦慢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果仗恃執著種種迷於五取蘊的錯誤思想，心生輕慢高舉，認為自己的思想是最第一的，最高尚的，這種迷於苦諦所生諸見引生的高慢心，稱為迷苦慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉十、由無明</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科由無明，由迷於苦諦而生無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有無智，與此諸見及疑、貪等煩惱相應，若唯於苦獨行無智，如是并名迷苦無明。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面說過無明有二種，一種是相應無明（共無明），一種是不相應無明（不共無明），相應無明是與煩惱相應的無明，不相應無明是無明單獨生起，不與十煩惱相應。若是沒有智慧的人，與這裡所說的薩迦耶見、邊執見、見取見、戒禁取見等種種見解及疑惑、貪取、瞋恚等煩惱相應，這是煩惱相應無明；若是這種煩惱是單獨對五取蘊不明白是苦的無智，這是煩惱不相應無明。這二種無明，一是相應無明，一是不相應無明，都是迷於苦諦所生的無明，稱為迷苦無明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、總結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總結，總結十種迷於苦諦的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4743"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此十煩惱皆迷苦諦，見苦所斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這十種煩惱都是迷惑於苦諦（五取蘊），見道位的時候所要斷除的煩惱，稱為見苦所斷。進入聖道的第一關，就是要斷除分別所起的、思想上的煩惱，上面所說貪恚慢無明的煩惱都是與錯誤的見（思想）相應而引起的，並不是俱生的煩惱所生，是屬於見道所斷的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》是迷苦貪至迷苦無明者：此中貪、恚、慢、無明，唯取一分。依見迷苦起者，是故此說見苦所斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處文中所說的貪、恚、慢、無明，只取一部分依迷於苦諦所生種種見而生起的煩惱，所以這裡說是見苦所斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、迷集2　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科迷集，說明迷於集諦的煩惱，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何迷集有八隨眠？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼迷於集諦有八種煩惱種子？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋2　申一、別辨4　酉一、由邪見2　戌一、辨5　亥一、謗因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科別辨，各別說明迷於集諦的煩惱，又分四科；第一科由邪見，由邪見迷於集諦（因為薩迦耶見、邊執見不屬迷於集諦的隨眠，所以不說明），又分二科；第一科辨，辨別迷於集諦生邪見的相貌，又分五科；第一科謗因，由迷於集諦生謗因邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂諸沙門、若婆羅門謗因邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有些沙門、婆羅門認為：一切樂果及苦果，都是沒有因的，稱為迷集的謗因邪見。如果沒有因，集是苦的因不成立，道是滅的因也不能成立了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、計自在等諸惡因論</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科計自在等諸惡因論，由迷於集諦，虛妄計執大自在天等諸惡因論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有沙門、若婆羅門，計自在等是一切物生者、化者及與作者，此惡因論所有邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有出家沙門或者是有學問的婆羅門，執著大自在天等是生出一切萬物的主宰者、是變化一切萬物的主宰者，以及是萬物的造作者，這些惡因論所有邪見，稱為迷集諦的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、謗無施愛等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科謗無施愛等，由迷於集諦毀謗無施無愛等。此處所說與前面迷苦諦的邪見有所不同，迷於集諦主要是，於生出五蘊的「因」上所生的迷惑，如果迷惑五蘊本身，稱為迷苦諦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有邪見，無施、無愛，亦無祠祀，無有妙行，亦無惡行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種邪見認為：無施與（布施沒有好的果報）、無愛樂（沒有功德等愛樂法可以尊重）、無祠祀（認為除了火天以外，三寶沒有什麼功德，不必以財食供養），沒有善行（善行沒有可愛的等流果及異孰果），亦無惡行（惡行沒有不可愛的等流果及異孰果），這些稱為迷集諦的謗因邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥四、不死矯亂一分</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科不死矯亂一分，不死矯亂一分也是迷於集諦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4744"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有邪見，不死矯亂外道沙門、若婆羅門所起一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種邪見，若有眾生請問集諦相關的問題，不死矯亂外道沙門、婆羅門，而矯亂回答，這稱為迷集諦的不死矯亂一分邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥五、謗集諦法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科謗集諦法，由迷於集諦，誹謗沒有集諦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有邪見，誹謗集諦。謂諸外道作如是計：如彼沙門喬答摩種，為諸弟子所說集諦，此定無有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種邪見，誹謗集諦。外道這樣想：如彼喬答摩種這個出家人（釋迦牟尼佛），為弟子所說的集諦，一定是沒有這回事的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結論，結說名迷集諦所起邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等見，是迷集諦所起邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上文所說種種見解，都是迷於集諦所起的邪見。緣起法是此有故彼有，事實上因果不能全然分割，迷於果也會迷於因，這些邪見都是對因果的錯誤認知，既迷於苦諦又迷於集諦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、由見取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由見取，由迷集諦生起見取見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有見取，取彼諸見以為第一，能得清淨、解脫、出離，是迷集諦所起見取。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若有見取見，取著這些錯誤的思想以為是第一的，能得到令心清淨、解脫煩惱、出離生死的因，這是迷於集諦所起的見取見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、由戒禁取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科戒禁取，由迷集諦生起戒禁取見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於隨順此見諸法所受戒禁，取為第一，能得清淨，廣說如前，是迷集諦戒禁取。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果隨順迷於集諦的邪見、見取見等種種法，所受的戒禁，身護語護等，認為這樣是最第一殊勝的，是令心清淨、解脫煩惱、出離生死的因，這是迷於集諦所起的戒禁取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能得清淨廣說如前者：謂如見取中說，能得清淨、解脫、出離。此亦如是，故指如前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能得清淨廣說如前，是指如見取中說，能得清淨、解脫煩惱、出離生死。此處也一樣，所以說如前所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、由疑等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科由疑等，由迷集諦生起疑等煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4745"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">餘疑、貪等，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面所說的應該知道，不同的是迷集諦而已。疑、貪及無明等，也都是迷於苦諦的因，對五取蘊的因所生的諸見，產生疑惑或貪著，稱為迷於集諦的疑和貪等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、總結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總結，總結八種迷於集諦的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是八種煩惱隨眠，迷於集諦，見集所斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上所說八種煩惱種子，是迷於集諦所生，是見集所斷。是見道時，觀察集諦所要斷除的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》餘疑貪等如前應知者：前說迷苦，說有疑、貪、恚、慢、無明。今說其相，當知亦爾。然此迷集，是其差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面所說迷於苦諦，而生疑、貪、恚、慢、無明，現在所說疑、貪、恚、慢、無明的煩惱相，都是同樣的解釋，不過一種是迷苦，迷於五取蘊，一種是迷集，迷於五取蘊之生因（煩惱及業），這是迷苦和迷集差別之處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、迷滅2　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科迷滅，說明迷於滅諦涅槃的煩惱，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何迷滅有八隨眠？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼說迷於滅諦也有八種煩惱種子？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋2　申一、別辨4　酉一、由邪見2　戌一、辨5　亥一、計邊無邊不死矯亂一分</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科別辨，各別說明，又分四科；第一科由邪見，由迷於滅諦生起邪見，又分二科；第一科辨，辨明邪見的相狀，又分五科；第一科計邊無邊不死矯亂一分，執著有邊、無邊，還有不死矯亂論的一部分，是屬於迷滅諦生起的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂諸沙門、若婆羅門，計邊無邊、不死矯亂諸見一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸外道出家沙門、婆羅門，對滅諦涅槃有錯誤的認知，因而執著有邊、無邊，還有不死矯亂論的一部分所生的邪見，這些都是迷於滅諦的所引起的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、計現法涅槃</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科計現法涅槃，由迷於滅諦，生起虛妄執著現法涅槃論的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有沙門、若婆羅門，謂說現法涅槃論者所有邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有沙門、若婆羅門，執著現在的色受想行識就可以得到涅槃，不用死了以後才能得到涅槃。他們執著的現法涅槃就是快樂，第一種，外道執著受用人天五欲的快樂，盡情享受色聲香味觸五欲就是涅槃；另外四種，外道執著初禪、二禪、三禪、四禪由禪定所生的快樂就是涅槃。這是對滅諦涅槃無知所生的邪見，屬迷於滅諦所生的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、撥無世間真阿羅漢3　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科撥無世間真阿羅漢，由迷於滅諦涅槃，生起撥無世間真阿羅漢的邪見，分三科；第一科標，標出邪見相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4746"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有邪見，撥無世間真阿羅漢，乃至廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種邪見，撥無世間真阿羅漢，乃至詳細如前所說謗滅諦法所生邪見等，這也是迷於滅諦涅槃所生的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼阿羅漢二德所顯，謂斷及智。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能夠證得阿羅漢，有二種功德梵行所顯示，一是斷德，二是智德。斷就是斷煩惱，《顯揚聖教論》卷3說煩惱斷有二種，一種是諸纏斷，斷煩惱的現行，一種是隨眠斷，斷煩惱的種子，永盡貪斷、永盡瞋斷、永盡癡斷，貪瞋癡三毒的種子永斷，才是阿羅漢。智，是指二種智，一種是盡智，一種是無生智。盡智是煩惱永盡，永遠不會再生起煩惱；無生智，因為沒有煩惱就沒有因了，沒有因將來不會得果，下一生不用再來三界得果報，所以是無生，不會再生起另外一個生命。阿羅漢有這二種功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科簡，簡取謗斷邪見為迷於滅諦所生邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中但取謗斷邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道沒有智慧，此處就不說智，只說阿羅漢斷煩惱的部分。若對阿羅漢斷盡煩惱成就涅槃的部分，有錯誤的思想邪見，稱為謗斷邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥四、謗滅諦法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科謗滅諦法，由迷於滅諦，生起撥無滅諦法的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有邪見，誹謗滅諦，謂諸外道，廣說如前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一種邪見，誹謗滅諦，是指外道認為佛說的涅槃是沒有的，詳細情形如前文所說可知。這也是屬於誹謗滅諦的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥五、橫計諸邪解脫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科橫計諸邪解脫，由迷於滅諦，生起橫計諸邪解脫的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有橫計諸邪解脫所有邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有外道由迷於滅諦涅槃，錯誤的執著解脫而生起邪見。例如認為生天是解脫等，也是屬於謗滅諦的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結說名迷滅諦所起邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是諸見，是迷滅諦所起邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上面所說的錯誤思想，是由於迷惑滅諦所生起的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂諸外道廣說如前者：前說外道誹謗苦諦及與集諦，起大邪見。彼謂沙門喬答摩種，為諸弟子施設苦諦、集諦，此定無有。今說誹謗滅諦亦爾，故說如前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說外道誹謗苦諦及與集諦，生起大邪見。他們認為沙門喬答摩種，為弟子所施設安立的苦諦、集諦是沒有的。現在誹謗滅諦也是一樣，也說滅諦是沒有的，所以說如前所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4747"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、由見取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由見取，由迷滅諦生見取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有見取，取彼諸見以為第一，廣說如前，是迷滅諦所起見取。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若有見取，執著以上所說的這些迷滅諦邪見思想是第一的，能清淨內心、解脫煩惱、出離生死，與前面所說的完全一樣，稱為迷滅諦所取的見取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》以為第一廣說如前者：謂如前說，能得清淨、解脫、出離，下亦準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前文所說，能得清淨、能解脫煩惱、出離生死，下文也可以準照前文所說而知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、由戒禁取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由戒禁取，由迷滅諦生戒禁取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於隨順彼見諸法所受戒禁，取為第一，廣說如前，是迷滅諦戒禁取。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道如果隨順迷於滅諦所生的種種邪見，認為應該要受什麼戒禁才能夠證得涅槃，而且認為這種戒禁是第一的，最殊勝的，能得內心清淨、解脫煩惱、出離生死，與前面所說的完全一樣，稱為迷滅諦的戒禁取。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、由餘貪等2　戌一、總標簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科由餘貪等，由迷滅諦生餘貪等煩惱，分二科；第一科總標簡，總相標示簡別瞋煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所餘貪等，如前應知，唯除瞋恚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所餘貪等煩惱，都是對於滅諦涅槃所生諸見生起貪等煩惱，與前文所說的一樣；唯除迷滅諦生起瞋心，這一點是不同的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、別釋相2　亥一、顯瞋恚</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋相，各別解釋迷滅諦生瞋恚的相狀，分二科；第一科顯瞋恚，顯出瞋恚的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於滅諦起怖畏心、起損害心、起恚惱心，如是瞋恚，迷於滅諦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於佛說的滅諦涅槃生起怖畏心：認為涅槃是我沒有了，我所有的身體沒有了，我的親戚朋友、我所愛的東西通通都沒有了，感覺很恐怖，生起損害心，生起瞋恚惱怒之心，對成就涅槃感覺到不快樂。這種瞋恚是迷於滅諦而生的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、餘例前</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科餘例前，其他的如前所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">餘如前說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其他的貪、慢、無明、疑，如同前面所說的不再多說了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、總結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總結，總結八種迷於滅諦的煩惱屬見滅所斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4748"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是八種煩惱隨眠，迷於滅諦，見滅所斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前所說有八種煩惱種子，迷於滅諦，是見道位時，見滅諦所要斷除的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》所餘貪等如前應知等者：前說迷苦、集諦，有疑、貪、恚、慢與無明。今此亦爾，唯除瞋恚迷相有別，餘如前說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面說迷苦、集諦，有疑、貪、恚、慢與無明產生。此處迷滅諦所生疑、貪、恚、慢與無明也是一樣，除瞋心的迷惑行相：對於涅槃生起怖畏心、損害心、恚惱心等相貌有所差別以外，其他像前面所說的一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、迷道2　未一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科迷道，說明迷於道諦生起的煩惱，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何迷道有八隨眠？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼樣說迷道諦有八種的煩惱種子？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋2　申一、別辨4　酉一、由邪見4　戌一、謗無世間真阿羅漢2　亥一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科別辨，各別說明迷於道諦生起的煩惱，又分四科；第一科由邪見，由迷於道諦生起邪見，又分四科；第一科謗無世間真阿羅漢，由迷於道諦生起謗無世間真阿羅漢的邪見，又分二科；第一科標，標出邪見相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂撥無世間真阿羅漢，乃至廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　毀謗世間沒有真阿羅漢，乃至如前文廣說，這是因為迷於道諦而生起邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中所有誹謗一切智為導首有為無漏，當知此見，是迷道諦所起邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　道諦是指三十七道品，是得到滅諦的智慧和方法，三十七道品都是以智慧為導首，能斷的智慧是有為的，無漏的，能使令有情得到阿羅漢果，外道認為沒有三十七道品，這種毀謗的邪見，稱為迷道諦所起的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、不死矯亂一分</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不死矯亂一分，不死矯亂一分也是迷於道諦所生的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又諸沙門、若婆羅門，不死矯亂邪見一分，亦迷於道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又諸外道出家沙門、婆羅門，有一分對於道諦不了解，而有不死矯亂的邪見，也是迷於道諦所生的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4749"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、謗道諦法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科謗道諦法，由迷於道諦生起謗無道諦法的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又諸外道謗道邪見，彼謂沙門喬答摩種，為諸弟子說出離道，實非出離，由此不能盡出離苦。佛所施設無我之見，及所受持戒禁隨法，是惡邪道，非正妙道。如是亦名迷道邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又外道毀謗道諦邪見，認為佛為弟子們說的出離道不是真的出離，三十七道品不是真的能令人得到涅槃，出離生死苦惱。佛所安立無我的見解及所受持的戒禁隨順涅槃之法，如五戒、八戒、八關齋戒、具足戒等，都是惡邪道，不是正確殊勝微妙的道諦，這種邪見也是迷於道諦、毀謗道諦法的一種邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、計惡邪道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科計惡邪見，由迷於道諦生起計惡邪見。</span></span></span></div>
