<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有第二種道理解釋我我所等煩惱是雜染品類。是指於通達身受心法等所知事無常苦空無我的實相，證入滅諦涅槃時，有二種法會產生極大的障礙。這二障是：邪行因緣、苦生因緣。邪行因緣，是指錯誤的身語意三業；苦生因緣，是指令苦生起的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、隨釋2　巳一、邪行因緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋二種障礙寂滅之法，又分二科；第一科邪行因緣，說明邪行因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">邪行因緣者，謂六十二見。因此執故，於諸有情由身語意起諸邪行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　邪行因緣方面，是指依止我見、我所見而生的六十二見，由於這六十二見的緣故，心中生起種種錯誤的虛妄分別，於其他的有情，由身體、語言、意念，生起種種錯誤的行為。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、苦生因緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科苦生因緣，不斷煩惱種子是苦生因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">苦生因緣者，謂不斷隨眠故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦生因緣方面，是指有情會不斷的有三界的生死苦，產生苦的因緣就是因為沒有斷除煩惱的種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋二因緣2　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋二因緣，解釋邪行及苦生二種因緣，分二科；第一科標，標出邪行及苦生因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此二法有二因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這種邪行因緣、苦生因緣都有各自生起的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋2　巳一、邪行因緣因緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，又分二科；第二科邪行因緣因緣，說明邪行因緣的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">邪行因緣因緣者，謂計我、我所薩迦耶見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　邪行因緣的因緣方面，是指執著有我、我所的薩迦耶見，使令有情對其他有情，造出種種身語意三業錯誤的行為，這是依六十二見生邪行因緣的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、苦生因緣因緣2　午一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科苦生因緣的因緣，說明苦生因緣的因緣，分二科；第一科標，標出苦生因緣的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4776"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">苦生因緣因緣者，謂初後兩位不起正行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦生因緣的因緣方面，是指於最初聽聞正法及最後修行時，這二種位次時，不能生起正確的身語意行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋不聞正法，不修正行是苦生因的緣因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由我慢故，初不聞正法；由增上慢故，後不修正行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為有高慢心，在初位不聽聞正法；由於有增上慢，認為自己有修行，事實上是錯認消息，因此在後位，沒有修正確的出離道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由增上慢故等者：此增上慢，義顯執著應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這增上慢，義理上顯示前文所說外道的執著心，應該知道。以為自己有修行，未證謂證，錯認消息，不對的也不如實探討，得禪定以為得聖道，或者顛倒聽法，這就是增上慢。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、第三義2　卯一、舉善說3　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第三義，依第三種道理解釋計我等所攝的煩惱雜染，分二科；第一科舉善說，舉出佛的經律論所說，分三科；第一科標，標出所說的法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有差別。謂於善說法毗奈耶中，有四種法為最、為上、勝極、勝妙、不共外道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以第三種道理解釋我我所等煩惱是雜染品類的差別。是指在佛說法的經律論當中，有四種法是最高的、最上等的、最殊勝的、最勝妙的、不共外道的，再沒有人能夠超越的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為四？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　哪四種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出四種不共外道之佛法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、於諦簡擇；二者、於己同梵行所，修可樂法；三者、於異論所不生憎嫉；四、於清淨品能不退失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛法的殊勝有四點。一於諦簡擇。於四聖諦簡別決擇世間及出世間的因果，使令有情依此通達諸法實相，證得我空，法空真理。於諦簡擇，從淺到深能成就世間人天福報的增上生道，及出世間三乘道果的決定勝道，這是外道所沒有的。二於己同梵行所，修可樂法。對於與自己在一起共同修行的同梵行所，修六和敬：見和同解、戒和同修、利和同均、意和同悅、口和無諍、身和同住。一同趣向決定勝道。像阿那律尊者在樹林裏與另外兩位比丘住在一起時，誰有空誰就將該做的事情完成，然後就各自修習善法，他們都是先想到他人，對同梵行者沒有高慢心，沒有互相嫉妒障礙，覺得與同梵行者一起修行是非常殊勝的。三於異論所不生憎嫉。於與自己不同思想處，不生憎恨嫉妒。佛教對與佛法不同的思想處，不會憎恨，也不會嫉妒，包容心很大。佛教對不同的思想都給予尊重，所以在歷史上只有佛教沒有發動戰爭，而其他的宗教都曾因為教義的衝突而發動戰爭。四於清淨品能不退失。清淨品就是清淨心，清淨心能不退失就是因為能夠斷除煩惱種子，這也是外道法門所沒有的。外道最多修到非想非非想定就很了不起了。以上這四點對佛法而言，是最殊勝，不共於外道的地方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、顯惡說2　辰一、舉四法2　巳一、略標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二點顯惡說，顯示外道邪見惡說，分二科；第一科舉四法，舉出惡說法也有四種，分二科；第一科略標列，要略標示出四種惡說法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4777"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於惡說法毗奈耶中，有四種法，於此四法極為障礙。一、計我、我所薩迦耶見，二、我慢，三、妄執諦取，四、不斷隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在外道的惡說法當中，有四種法，對於前文所說的四種不共外道殊勝的佛法之修習，會形成很大的障礙。一計我、我所薩迦耶見，執著有我見，有我所見，於諦的簡擇有所障礙；二我慢，有我慢心對於與自己一起修行的同梵行者，不會可樂，不能和合，因為自覺得了不起，或者是有一種殊勝感，優越感，這樣的人，不能對同梵行者修六和敬等可愛樂法；三妄執諦取，虛妄執取出離道，錯誤的認識諸法實相，而且執著甚深，有邪見，使令他們於異論所產生憎妒，佛法與他們說的不一樣，對於四諦不能承認，覺得佛說的不是真實的。四不斷隨眠，外道法不能斷除煩惱的種子，對於所修的清淨品就會退失。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷16：景法師說：一計我我所者，障前四中第二於已同梵行所修可樂法；二我慢者，障前第三於異論所不生增嫉，由有我慢於諸異論多生憎嫉。三妄執諦取者，障前第一於諦簡擇，四不斷隨眠者，障前第四於清淨品能不退失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、隨難釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨難釋，隨著困難的地方再加以解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此因緣，雖到有頂，必還墮落。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為外道有這些煩惱，雖然修到非想非非想處天的三界之頂，將來也還是會墮落到下地欲界、色界，還是在三界輪迴。這是第三義說明我我所見等煩惱是染汙煩惱品類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、舉二執2　巳一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科舉二執，舉出二種執著，分二科；第一科略標，要略標出二種執著。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有二執。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有二種執著。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、列釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列釋，列舉出二種執著並解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、根、境執，謂執我、我所。二、展轉有情執，謂我慢，計我為勝等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道法還有二種執著。一、根、境執，謂執我、我所。根是指眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意六根；境是指色、聲、香、味、觸、法外六境，外道執著生命體的內六根是我，執著外六塵是我所。二、展轉有情執，謂我慢，計我為勝等。展轉有情執是依有情自己興盛的事與其他有情之間由劣、等、勝的差別，展轉比較而生起高慢心的執著，執著自己勝過他人或執著自己比他人少分下劣等，如前文所說七慢或九慢等。外道有根執、境執及展轉有情執，這二種執著，對內六根、外六境、有情都有執著，一切法不會超過有情與器世間，換句話說，就是對一切法都有執著。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》計我為勝等者：此中等言，等取計我為等、為劣應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面曾說過七種慢，此中等字，應該知道是指計度執著我與他人相等，或是我比他人差等的情況所顯的慢心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子五、欲為苦因攝2　丑一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科欲為苦因攝，會經說欲為苦因所攝，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：自有貪愛為眾苦因，何故餘處世尊復說欲為苦因？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：前文說貪愛是集諦，自心所有的貪愛是眾苦的原因，為什麼其他的經律論中，佛還要說欲是苦的原因？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、答3　寅一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科標，標出欲是苦的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：以是現法苦因緣故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：因為欲是令有情現在的生命體受苦的因緣，所以佛說欲也是苦因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4778"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼原因？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋欲是現法苦的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於有情有欲、有貪、或有親昵，彼若變異，便生憂惱等苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果對於其他有情有欲望、有貪心、或有親暱貪，想要親近這種欲，有這些男女欲，如果對方有變化，變心了或者生病了，心裏就憂愁苦惱，因此說欲是使令有情現在生命體產生苦的原因，這裡特別強調是現法的苦因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子六、龜駝等攝7　丑一、說龜喻</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科龜駝等攝，會諸經所說龜駝等喻煩惱雜染，分七科；第一科說龜喻，用烏龜來譬喻煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故五蓋說名為龜？答：五支相似故，能障修習如理作意故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為何用烏龜來比喻五蓋的煩惱？答：五蓋是貪欲，瞋恚，昏沈掉舉，惡作睡眠和疑等煩惱，這好像烏龜的五個支幹：四條腿一個頭一樣。另外這五蓋將有情清淨的心覆蓋住，能夠障礙有情修習如理作意，所以經典用烏龜來比喻五蓋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　註：五蓋喻為龜，於北傳：《雜阿含》1079經，別譯《雜阿含》18經，《增壹阿含》39品9經；南傳：《中部》23經都有這個譬喻。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、說母駝喻</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科說母駝喻，以母駝譬喻煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何緣故忿說名母駝？答：似彼性故，由惡語者，於他言詞不能堪忍增上力故，能障得彼教授教誡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為何說忿怒就像母駝？母駝這一種動物，惡意嚼草，牠吃東西的時候，好像心裏很生氣的樣子。答：因為忿怒就像脾氣很不好的母駝一樣，有惡口的人，於他人來告誡時，一點也沒有忍耐力，出言不遜，因此他人不敢去勸諫，能障礙惡口者得到善知識的教授、教誡。母駝就是形容憤怒的心，憤怒的煩惱譬喻母駝。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、說凝血喻</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科說凝血喻，說凝血譬喻煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故慳、嫉說名凝血？答：由於虛薄無味利養而現行故，能障可愛樂法故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為何說慳、嫉稱為凝血？答：慳貪，嫉妒，就像剛入胎藏時凝固的凝血，脆弱不耐碰觸，名羯羅藍，又名凝血一樣，由於對虛薄無味的利養產生愛著，當他人獲得利養時，心生不忍，不耐他榮而生慳貪、嫉妒的煩惱，有這種煩惱能障礙他於同梵行所修六和敬等可愛樂法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、說机肉喻</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科說机肉喻，說屠机上肉譬喻諸欲的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故諸欲說名屠机上肉？答：繫屬主宰無定實故，能障無間修善法故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼說欲望就好像屠夫砧板上的肉？答：因為屠夫砧板上的肉不一定是屬於誰的，諸家共有，誰有錢誰就可以買走，大家都想爭這塊肉，就會產生爭執，種種的煩惱因此而生。欲也是一樣，不一定屬於誰，也不是真實有的，若內心對於諸家共有的欲生起貪愛，就會障礙、中斷有情相續修習善法。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4779"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑五、說狼者喻</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科說狼者喻，說狼譬喻煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故無明說名狼者？答：似彼性故，障聞智故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼說無明像狼？答：因為無明就像狼一樣極為癡鈍，障礙有情得到聞法的智慧。《瑜伽論記》神泰法師說：狼也名為鼠狼，蛇想要吃牠的時候呢，牠就用尾巴障礙蛇的口，蛇就不能吃牠了，如同無明障於文字不得聞法，所以用狼來比喻障礙聞慧。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑六、說岐路喻</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科說岐路喻，說岐路譬喻煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何緣故疑說名岐路？答：似彼性故，障思智故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼懷疑，佛比喻成歧路？答：因為歧路是有好幾條路接在一起，東邊一條、西邊一條、前面一條、後面還有一條，不知道要走那一條路才對。於佛法心懷猶豫，不能決定就像歧路一樣，能障礙有情得到思惟的智慧，令有情思惟佛法時不能生起決定的勝解，所以疑、不決定性就用岐路來比喻。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑七、說輪圍喻</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科說輪圍喻，說輪圍山譬喻煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故我慢說名輪圍？答：似彼性故，障修智故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼我慢，佛比喻成輪圍？答：因為我慢就像輪圍山一樣，難可越度，障礙有情修行的智慧，難以突破我慢高山的障礙，所以用輪圍山來比喻我慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子七、貪瞋等攝2　丑一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科貪瞋等攝，會經所說貪瞋等所攝的煩惱雜染，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：更有所餘能發惡行無量煩惱，何故簡取貪瞋癡，立不善根？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：還有其他的煩惱使令有情產生身語意的惡行，產生無量的煩惱，為什麼只將貪瞋癡三法簡別取出，安立為不善根？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、答2　寅一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標，標出貪瞋等發業因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：發業因緣略有三種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：使令有情產生錯誤的身語意邪業的因緣，要略而言有三種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋三種發業因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂愛味因緣故，損他因緣故，執著建立邪法因緣故。此貪瞋癡於上因緣，如應配釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　愛味因緣、損他因緣、執著建立邪法因緣，這三種因緣，是使令有情產生錯誤的身語意邪業的因緣。愛味因緣使有情生貪，損他因緣使有情生瞋，執著建立邪法因緣使有情生癡，由貪瞋癡產生這三種發業因緣。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="58p4780"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、嗢柁南結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科嗢柁南結，以偈結說會諸經所說的煩惱雜染，主要是針對前面這一段的要義重新整理回顧以偈頌表示，安置在文的中間，稱為中嗢柁南。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中嗢柁南曰：</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲愛離欲　計我等欲　龜母駝等　及貪瞋等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《披尋記》的作者很善巧，用偈頌來分科。以偈頌標出欲貪、貪愛、離欲、計我等、欲為苦因、龜駝等、貪瞋等攝七科。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲愛離欲：包括欲貪、貪愛、離欲攝三科。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　計我等欲：包括計我等、欲為苦因二科。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　龜母駝等：包括龜駝等一科。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　及貪瞋等：包括貪瞋等攝一科。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由以上是欲愛等將諸經所說的煩惱雜染作詳細的說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第五十八</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div style="border-radius:0px; width:24px !important">&nbsp;</div>
</div>
